### [203] [Beyond Runtime Enforcement: Shield Synthesis as Defensibility Analysis for Adversarial Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13621)
*Achraf Hsain,Sultan Almuhammadi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出屏蔽强化学习不应作为运行时安全机制，而应作为设计时分析工具。通过构建受约束的两玩家安全博弈进行网络防御，形式化地输出"可防御性裁决"及"可防御性指纹"，揭示系统的结构性安全属性而非策略约束。实验表明形式可防御性与操作有效性解耦，屏蔽合成更适合回答架构层面的安全问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反驳屏蔽强化学习作为运行时安全机制的主流观点，指出自动机理论工具（规范编译、乘积博弈构建、吸引子计算、胜区提取）更适合作为设计时分析工具，用于获取系统的结构性洞见而非运行时约束。

Method: 构建受约束的两玩家安全博弈：防御者规范定义不安全区域，攻击者规范限制对手合法动作。通过吸引子计算和胜区提取求解博弈，得到可防御性裁决。进一步从吸引子结构推导拓扑级指标，结合屏蔽约束下的多智能体对抗强化学习行为，构建可防御性指纹。

Result: 形式可防御性与操作有效性在安全评估中解耦：小的架构变化可导致操作结果大幅变化而形式安全边际几乎不变。可防御性指纹同时捕获了网络的形式安全属性和自适应博弈下的操作行为。

Conclusion: 屏蔽合成最有价值的应用不是作为安全智能体的部署机制，而是作为回答架构层面安全问题的框架：系统是否可防御、何处可防御、如何可防御。可防御性裁决（而非安全策略）才是核心输出。

Abstract: Shielded reinforcement learning is typically presented as a runtime safety mechanism that compiles temporal-logic specifications into automata restricting an agent's actions. We argue this is the wrong product. The same automata-theoretic machinery -- specification compilation, product game construction, attractor computation, and winning-region extraction -- is better read as a design-time analytical instrument whose outputs are structural insights about a system rather than runtime constraints on a deployed agent.
  We instantiate this through a constrained two-player safety game for network defense. The two specifications are enforced asymmetrically: the defender specification defines the unsafe region of the game, whereas the attacker specification restricts the adversary's legal actions during attractor computation. Solving the game yields a defensibility verdict -- a formal certificate that a topology-specification pair is or is not defensible -- with the associated winning region and shield.
  Beyond the binary verdict, we derive topology-level metrics from the attractor structure and combine them with post-convergence behavior from shield-constrained adversarial multi-agent reinforcement learning. Together these form a defensibility fingerprint capturing both a network's formal safety properties and its operational behavior under adaptive play.
  A what-if analysis shows that formal defensibility and operational effectiveness capture distinct aspects of security: small architectural changes can produce large shifts in operational outcomes while leaving formal safety margins nearly unchanged. Shield synthesis is thus most valuable not as a deployment mechanism for safe agents, but as a framework for answering architectural questions about whether, where, and how a system can be defended. The defensibility verdict is the output, not the safe policy.

</details>


### [204] [Before You Think: System 0, AI-Mediated Cognition and Cognitive Colonization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13658)
*Marianna Bergamaschi Ganapini,Massimo Chiriatti,Enrico Panai,Giuseppe Riva*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文考察了三种理解人工智能认知与认识论后果的框架——三系统理论、思维框架和系统0，论证系统0具有独特的理论地位，并引入"认知殖民化"概念，揭示AI系统如何将外部利益嵌入自我架构，形成难以被用户察觉的隐性影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有框架（三系统理论、思维框架）虽然捕捉了AI对个体推理和集体认识论实践的重要维度，但未能充分解释AI系统嵌入自我架构的隐性影响机制，亟需一个新的理论视角来理解这种广泛部署但难以察觉的认知后果。

Method: 通过对三系统理论、思维框架和系统0三种理论框架的比较分析，论证系统0的独特理论地位，并在此基础上提出"认知殖民化"这一新的理论概念。

Result: 发现系统0在三者中占据独特理论地位，前两种框架无法完全复制其解释力；提出了"认知殖民化"概念以描述AI系统将外部利益嵌入自我认知架构的机制。

Conclusion: 由于AI系统已广泛部署，理解这些不可见的认知影响力形式是紧迫的哲学与实践任务。

Abstract: This paper examines three recent frameworks for understanding the cognitive and epistemic consequences of artificial intelligence: Tri-System Theory, Thinkframes, and System 0. It argues that while the first two capture important dimensions of AI's influence on individual reasoning and collective epistemic practices, System 0 occupies a theoretically distinctive position that neither can fully replicate. The paper introduces the concept of cognitive colonization, according to which AI systems can embed external interests within the architecture of the self in ways that are difficult for users to perceive. Because such systems are already widely deployed, understanding these invisible forms of influence is an urgent philosophical and practical task.

</details>


### [205] [EurekAgent: Agent Environment Engineering is All You Need For Autonomous Scientific Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13662)
*Amy Xin,Jiening Siow,Junjie Wang,Zijun Yao,Fanjin Zhang,Jian Song,Lei Hou,Juanzi Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出环境工程（Environment Engineering）是自主科学发现的关键瓶颈，并设计了EurekAgent系统，通过权限、工件、预算和人机协同四维环境工程设计，在数学、内核工程和机器学习任务上取得SOTA结果，包括以不到11美元API成本发现26-圆填充新SOTA结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着LLM代理能力持续提升，自主科学发现的瓶颈正从设计代理工作流转向设计代理环境（资源、约束和接口）。当前缺乏系统化的环境工程方法论来引导代理行为、抑制奖励黑客等有害行为。

Method: 提出EurekAgent系统，通过四维环境工程设计：1) 权限工程（权限工程）：有界代理执行与隔离评估；2) 工件工程（工件工程）：基于文件系统和Git的协作；3) 预算工程（预算工程）：预算感知的探索；4) 人机协同工程（人机协同工程）：便捷的人工监督与干预。

Result: 在多个数学、内核工程和机器学习任务上取得新SOTA结果，包括以不到11美元总API成本发现26-圆填充新SOTA结果。

Conclusion: 自主科学发现的瓶颈正转向环境工程，应将环境工程作为开发可靠自主研究代理的核心研究方向。代码和结果已开源。

Abstract: LLM-based agents have shown increasing potential in automating scientific discovery. Given an optimizable metric and an execution environment, they can propose, validate, and iterate scientific solutions, and have produced results that outperform human-designed approaches. As model capabilities continue to improve, we argue that the bottleneck for autonomous scientific discovery is shifting from prescribing agent workflows to designing agent environments: the resources, constraints, and interfaces that shape agent behavior. We frame this as environment engineering: building environments that amplify productive behaviors, such as open-ended exploration, systematic artifact management, and inter-agent collaboration, while suppressing harmful behaviors, such as reward hacking and high-friction human oversight. We present EurekAgent, an environment-engineered agent system for metric-driven autonomous scientific discovery. EurekAgent engineers the environment along four dimensions: permissions engineering for bounded agent execution and isolated evaluation; artifact engineering for filesystem and Git-based collaboration; budget engineering for budget-aware exploration; and human-in-the-loop engineering for easy human supervision and intervention. EurekAgent sets new state-of-the-art results on multiple mathematics, kernel engineering, and machine learning tasks, including new state-of-the-art 26-circle packing results discovered with less than $11 in total API cost. We open-source our code and results, and call for environment engineering as a core research direction for developing reliable autonomous research agents.

</details>


### [206] [Agents-K1: Towards Agent-native Knowledge Orchestration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13669)
*Zongsheng Cao,Bihao Zhan,Jinxin Shi,Jiong Wang,Fangchen Yu,Zhijie Zhong,Zijie Guo,Tianshuo Peng,Zhuo Liu,Yi Xie,Xiang Zhuang,Yue Fan,Runmin Ma,Shiyang Feng,Xiangchao Yan,Anran Liu,Peng Ye,Wenlong Zhang,Shufei Zhang,Chunfeng Song,Fenghua Ling,Jie Zhou,Liang He,Bo Zhang,Lei Bai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Agents-K1 是一个端到端的科学知识编排管线，将原始论文转化为智能体原生知识图谱。该管线包含多模态解析器、基于GRPO训练的4B信息抽取骨干网络和三元组智能体接口。基于此构建了涵盖246万篇论文的Scholar-KG知识图谱，在科学信息抽取、知识图谱构建和多跳科学推理方面表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的研究智能体虽然通过智能体编排取得了进展，但严重忽视了科学知识编排，通常将论文简化为摘要、表面提及和扁平引用边，忽略了科学推理所需的关键实体、论点、证据、机制和方法谱系。

Method: 提出Agents-K1管线，包含三个组件：1) 五模块多模态解析器，覆盖全文（而非仅摘要）的实体、多模态证据、引用和类型化实体间关系；2) 基于GRPO和规则奖励训练的4B信息抽取骨干网络；3) graph-anything CLI三元组智能体接口，统一网络搜索、多模态图谱检索和跨文档遍历。

Result: 基于该管线处理了六个学科246万篇科学论文，构建Scholar-KG，并开源100万论文子集。实验表明Agents-K1在科学信息抽取、知识图谱构建和多跳科学推理中取得优异性能。

Conclusion: Agents-K1通过科学知识编排显著提升了研究智能体的推理能力，该管线可扩展至通用领域语料库和符合模式的数据合成。

Abstract: Current LLM-based research agents have advanced through agent orchestration, yet largely overlook scientific knowledge orchestration. Existing works often reduce papers to abstracts, surface mentions, and flat \texttt{cites} edges, omitting key entities, claims, evidence, mechanisms, and method lineages essential for scientific reasoning. To this end, we introduce \textbf{Agents-K1}, an end-to-end knowledge orchestration pipeline that converts raw documents into agent-native scientific knowledge graphs. Agents-K1 integrates three components under a unifying theoretical foundation: a multimodal parser whose five-module schema captures entities, multimodal evidence, citations, and typed inter-entity relations across the full paper rather than abstracts alone; a 4B information-extraction backbone trained with GRPO under a rule-based reward; and a graphanything CLI, a tri-source agent interface that unifies web search, multimodal graph retrieval, and cross-document traversal. On top of this, we process 2.46 million scientific papers across six subjects to produce \textbf{Scholar-KG}, of which we release a one-million-paper subset, and the full Scholar-KG is accessible via the SCP link below. The same pipeline can be extended to general-domain corpora and to schema-conformant data synthesis. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Agents-K1 achieves superior performance in scientific information extraction, knowledge graph construction, and multi-hop scientific reasoning.

### [207] [Automated reproducibility assessments in the social and behavioral sciences using large language models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13670)
*Tobias Holtdirk,Pietro Marcolongo,Anna Steinberg Schulten,Felix Henninger,Stefan Rose,Sarah Ball,Bolei Ma,Frauke Kreuter,Markus Weinmann,Stefan Feuerriegel*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究证明大型语言模型（LLMs）可以自动化评估社会和 behavioral 科学研究的可重复性。在76项已发表研究中，LLM管道以±0.05的Cohen's d容差恢复了41%的原始效应量，并在96%的案例中得出与原始研究一致的定性结论，优于人类再分析者的34%和74%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的可重复性评估依赖独立研究人员重新分析原始数据，这种方法资源密集且难以规模化。因此，需要一种可扩展的自动化工具来系统评估实证结果的可重复性。

Method: 使用N=76项已发表的行为和社会科学研究，通过LLM生成分析结果，与原始发现和人类再分析结果进行比较。LLM管道计算效应量估计值，并以±0.05的Cohen's d容差评估与原始效应量的一致性，同时判断定性结论是否与原始研究一致。

Result: 7项研究LLM无法产生可行的效应量估计。在剩余研究中，LLM管道在41%的研究中恢复了原始效应量（±0.05容差），在96%的案例中得出与原始研究相同的定性结论。相比之下，人类再分析者恢复了34%的原始效应量，并在74%的案例中得出相同定性结论。

Conclusion: LLMs可以作为可扩展的自动化可重复性评估工具，为社会科学和行为科学实证结果的系统审计提供基础。

Abstract: Reproducibility in the social and behavioral sciences is typically evaluated by independent researchers who reanalyze the original data to assess whether the published findings can be recovered. However, such approaches are resource-intensive and difficult to scale. Here, we show that large language models (LLMs) can automate reproducibility assessments. Using N=76 published studies with predefined claims from the behavioral and social sciences, we compare LLM-generated analysis with the original findings and human reanalysis. For 7 studies, the LLM could not produce a viable effect size estimate. For the remaining studies, our LLM pipeline recovered the original effect sizes in 41% of studies using a +/-0.05 tolerance in Cohen's d. Further, our LLM pipeline reached the same qualitative conclusion as the original study in 96% of cases, where conclusions indicate whether the reanalysis supports the original claim. For comparison, human reanalysts recovered the original effect sizes in 34% of studies and reached the same qualitative conclusion in 74% of cases. Together, these results show that LLMs can serve as a scalable tool for automated reproducibility assessment and provide a foundation for systematic auditing of empirical results in the social and behavioral sciences.

</details>

### [208] [Characterizing Tests in IoT Software: Practices, Challenges and Opportunities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12592)
*Rufeng Chen,Hengcheng Zhu,Wuqi Zhang,Zixu Zhou,Lili Wei*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文首次对开源IoT软件的测试用例进行了实证研究，发现尽管IoT软件通常包含大量测试，但其有效性有限；主要挑战在于管理复杂的外部依赖交互，而Mock对象的使用与这些挑战高度吻合，表明Mock是提升测试覆盖率的潜在解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IoT软件缺陷可能导致严重后果（如智能门锁被非法入侵），但现有研究缺乏对IoT软件测试实践的系统性了解。为填补这一空白，作者开展了首个针对开源IoT软件测试用例的实证研究。

Method: 对开源IoT软件的测试用例进行实证研究：评估测试用例的有效性，探索测试挑战，分析Mock对象的使用情况。

Result: 1）IoT软件虽包含大量测试，但有效性有限；2）主要测试挑战是管理复杂的外部依赖（网络组件、文件系统、操作系统、数据库等）的交互；3）Mock对象的使用与所识别测试挑战高度一致。

Conclusion: Mock对象在IoT软件测试中的使用与测试挑战高度吻合，表明Mock是增强测试覆盖率和应对IoT软件测试复杂性的有效手段。

Abstract: The Internet of Things (IoT) is experiencing rapid growth. Smart devices are emerging in smart homes and industrial applications, performing mission-critical tasks. Bugs in IoT software can lead to severe consequences. For example, a buggy smart lock can allow unauthorized access to a private property. Testing is a primary practice to expose software bugs and ensure software quality. However, little is known about how IoT software is tested. To bridge this gap, we conducted the first empirical study on test cases in open-source IoT software. Specifically, we evaluated the effectiveness of test cases in IoT software, explored the challenges inherent in testing IoT software, and analyzed the usage of mock objects. Our results indicate that while IoT software often contains a considerable number of tests, their effectiveness remains limited. We identified the primary challenges in testing IoT software as managing complex interactions with various external dependencies, such as other network-reliant IoT components, file systems, operating systems, and databases. We also observed that the use of mock objects in IoT software closely aligns with our identified testing challenges. This alignment demonstrates the potential of mocking as a solution to enhance test coverage and address the complexities of IoT software testing.

*Luke Patterson,Li Wang,Adam Faulkner*

Main category: cs.SE

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准多基于纯学术 LeetCode 风格问题，且假设代码片段完全由人或 AI 编写，无法反映工业代码库中 AI 与人类代码混合的实际场景。为风险管理与生产力分析，需要更真实的细粒度检测基准。

Method: 基于 CodeSearchNet 构建包含人类与 AI 代码行级交错混合的 Python 文件数据集；在行级和块级两种粒度上，评估两种 SOTA AI 代码检测算法（AIGCode Detector 等）的性能。

Result: AIGCode Detector 在块级任务上最高 F1 为 0.48，行级任务上最高 F1 为 0.56，表明现有算法在该混合代码检测基准上仍有较大提升空间。

Abstract: Thanks to the rapid adoption of AI code assistants powered by large language models (LLMs), industry codebases are, increasingly, a hybrid of AI- and human-authored code. For risk management and productivity analysis purposes, it is crucial to enable fine-grained location detection of AI-generated code. To develop algorithms for this task, quality benchmarks are needed to assess performance. However, existing benchmarks tend to comprise academic, LeetCode-style problems and presume a code snippet is either completely human-authored or completely AI-authored, which is not reflective of the diverse intents and styles of industry codebases utilizing AI code assistants. To fill these gaps, we introduce HybridCodeAuthorship, a novel benchmark of Python code files with interleaved human- and AI-authored lines of code to simulate authentic utilization of AI code assistants. In this paper, we first present our dataset construction pipeline, which leverages CodeSearchNet, a massive collection of links to open sourced repositories on GitHub. We then benchmark the performance of two state-of-the-art AI-generated code detection algorithms at both the line- and chunk-level. Experimental results demonstrate that HybridCodeAuthorship is a challenging benchmark with a top-scoring algorithm, AIGCode Detector, obtaining a highest F1 score of 0.48 and 0.56 on chunk-level and line-level code detection tasks, respectively.

### [210] [Beyond Problem Solving: UOJ-Bench for Evaluating Code Generation, Hacking, and Repair in Competitive Programming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12864)
*Tingqiang Xu,Hangrui Zhou,Tianle Cai,Alex Gu,Kaifeng Lyu*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出UOJ-Bench基准，评估LLM在编程学习中的代码生成、错误识别（hacking）和代码修复能力。结果显示，最强模型一次评估无法识别超50%的错误提交，测试时扩展可提升至90%以上但计算成本高；最优模型能发现约30道题目中5%以上满分提交的错误，表明前沿LLM可补充传统判题系统的盲区。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在竞赛编程中表现强劲，但其在支持人类学习方面的作用尚未被探索，尤其是识别人类代码错误这一关键教育活动缺乏系统评估。

Method: 构建UOJ-Bench基准，包含代码生成、代码hacking（识别错误）和代码修复三个任务，数据来自UOJ真实提交，使用UOJ原生评测系统评估。

Result: 一次评估下最强模型无法识别超50%的错误提交；测试时扩展可将成功率提升至90%以上但计算成本高；最优模型能发现约30道题中5%以上满分提交中的隐藏错误。

Conclusion: LLM在编程教育辅助方面有潜力，尤其能发现传统判题系统遗漏的错误，但当前精度和计算成本限制其大规模部署。

Abstract: Despite strong performance in competitive programming, the role of Large Language Models (LLMs) in supporting human learning in the same setting remains largely unexplored. In this work, we introduce UOJ-Bench, a benchmark designed to evaluate not only the problem-solving ability of LLMs, but also their ability to identify errors in human-written code -- a crucial educational activity traditionally supported by running test cases over online judge systems. UOJ-Bench consists of three distinct tasks: code generation, code hacking, and code repair, all constructed from real-world code submissions on the Universal Online Judge (UOJ) and evaluated through UOJ's native judging infrastructure. Our results show that under one-shot evaluation, even the strongest models fail to identify errors in more than 50% of a set of submissions that have been found to be incorrect by UOJ users. While test-time scaling improves success rates to above 90%, the substantial computational costs incurred from model inference limit its practicality for large-scale deployment. Despite these limitations, we find that the best-performing models under test-time scaling can uncover errors in over 5% of full-score submissions across roughly 30 problems, suggesting that frontier LLMs can already provide complementary signals beyond standard judging systems.

Motivation: GenAI和LLM正在根本性地重塑软件工程，但缺乏系统性的综述来整合分散的研究证据，以理解其对实践、教育和劳动力的多维度影响。

Method: 采用四智能体研究流程（文献发现、科学计量分析、课程转型、劳动力影响），从软件工程、机器学习、计算教育、人-AI协作和软件生产力等顶级会议中筛选并分析了48篇经过验证的高影响力同行评审出版物。

Result: 发现2022年底后LLM-for-SE的年产出增长了约五倍；识别了九大主题和三条轨迹（实践、教育、劳动力）；证据在生产力效应的方向和程度上存在内部矛盾，表明收益高度依赖上下文。

Conclusion: AI原生软件工程的核心挑战在于培养工程师的判断力、验证和编排能力，而非单纯的代码生产能力；提出了概念框架、能力模型、课程路线图、教师发展与劳动力转型策略及11项研究议程。

Abstract: Generative Artificial Intelligence (GenAI), Large Language Models (LLMs), and emerging Agentic AI constitute the most disruptive transformation in the history of software engineering (SE), reshaping development processes, required competencies, professional roles, and the educational outcomes that universities must deliver. This paper presents a systematic review of 48 verified, influential peer-reviewed publications (2016--2026) drawn from leading venues in software engineering, machine learning, computing education, human--AI collaboration, and software productivity. Studies were discovered, screened, and analyzed through a four-agent research workflow (Literature Discovery, Scientometric Analysis, Curriculum Transformation, and Workforce Impact) and were verified against primary sources. We synthesize the evidence along nine themes and three trajectories -- practice, education, and workforce -- and report a scientometric inflection in which annual LLM-for-SE output grew roughly five-fold after late 2022. From this synthesis we contribute: (i) a conceptual framework for AI-native software engineering organized around \emph{intent}, \emph{collaboration}, and \emph{verification}; (ii) a nine-dimension competency model spanning specification, critical evaluation, agent orchestration, and metacognition; (iii) a four-phase university curriculum roadmap with AI-resilient assessment; (iv) faculty-development and workforce-transformation strategies; and (v) a prioritized agenda of eleven research gaps. The evidence base is internally contradictory on the magnitude and direction of productivity effects, underscoring that benefits are strongly context-dependent and that educating engineers for judgment, verification, and orchestration -- rather than code production alone -- is the central challenge of the AI-native era.

</details>


### [212] [The End of Code Review: Coding Agents Supersede Human Inspection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13175)
*Martin Monperrus*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文论证编码智能体（基于LLM的自主系统）已达到使传统人工代码审查不再必要的能力阈值，能够以更低成本、更高吞吐量满足代码审查的所有目标，且人工强制审查既无法提供有效保证也难以扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质疑并挑战软件工程中沿用五十年的人工代码审查作为必要质量关卡的传统观念，提出在编码智能体能力突破的当下，应重新审视人工审查的必要性。

Method: 通过两个核心论点进行论证：（1）代码审查的所有目标均可由智能体以更低成本和更高吞吐量实现；（2）智能体写代码+人工强制审查的简单结合模式是死胡同，既无实质保证也无法扩展。

Result: 提出编码智能体已跨越能力阈值，传统人工代码审查不再是软件质量管线的必要组成部分。

Conclusion: 建议摒弃人工强制审查模式，转向以智能体为中心的软件质量保障体系。

Abstract: Code review has been the primary quality gate in software development since Fagan formalised code inspection in 1976. For five decades, having a human examine and comment on a colleague's changes before merge has been a cornerstone practice at organisations of every size. Coding agents are large language model (LLM)-based autonomous systems capable of reading, writing, testing, and repairing software. We argue that coding agents have crossed a threshold of capability at which traditional human code review is no longer a necessary component of a software quality pipeline. Our argument rests on two claims: every stated goal of code review can be served by agents at lower cost and higher throughput; the naive integration in which agents write code and humans remain the mandatory reviewers is a dead end because it neither provides meaningful assurance nor scales with AI-assisted throughput.

TL;DR: 本文提出COM-as-Action范式，将专业软件交互从视觉控制重构为确定性程序合成，构建了工业CAD基准ComCADBench，并开发了自纠正智能体ComActor，在长期任务中显著优于GUI方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有计算机使用智能体在专业软件操作中存在根本性局限：基于GUI的方法面临脆弱的视觉定位和长程错误累积，基于API的方法则受限于异构协议和不可访问的商业接口。

Method: 提出COM-as-Action范式，利用组件对象模型作为统一可执行抽象；构建ComCADBench基准；开发ComActor自纠正智能体，采用渐进三阶段训练框架；构建ComForge可扩展训练平台。

Result: 前沿闭源模型在GUI交互下接近零成功率，而COM方法带来显著提升；ComActor在ComCADBench上达到SOTA，在长程任务中基线方法崩溃时仍保持强鲁棒性，并能泛化到外部CAD基准。

Conclusion: COM-as-Action范式有效弥合了语法正确性与几何精度之间的差距，为专业软件自动化提供了新的可行方向。

Abstract: Existing computer-use agents remain fundamentally limited in professional software manipulation: GUI-based agents suffer from fragile visual grounding and long-horizon error accumulation, while API-basedapproaches struggle with heterogeneous protocols and inaccessible commercial interfaces. In this work,we identify the Component Object Model (COM) as a unified executable abstraction, proposing COM-as-Action: a new paradigm that reframes professional software interaction as deterministic program synthesisrather than sequential visual control. To validate this paradigm in the most demanding environments, weintroduce ComCADBench, the first benchmark for agents operating real industrial CAD software. Ourexperiments reveal a substantial paradigm gap: frontier proprietary models achieve near-zero successunder GUI-based interaction, whereas COM-based execution yields substantial immediate gains. Tobridge the remaining gap between syntactic correctness and geometric accuracy, we develop ComActor, aself-correcting agent trained through a progressive three-stage framework, alongside ComForge, a scalableplatform for large-scale training in Windows containers. Extensive experiments show that ComActorachieves state-of-the-art performance on ComCADBench, with strong resilience in long-horizon taskswhere baselines collapse, and generalizes to external CAD benchmark.

### [214] [Mining Architectural Quality Under Agentic AI Adoption: A Causal Study of Java Repositories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13298)
*Oliver Aleksander Larsen,Mahyar T. Moghaddam*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 通过对151个开源Java仓库（74个采用AI编码工具，77个倾向性匹配对照）进行13个月的因果分析，发现AI编码工具并未显著改变架构坏味总数（+1.1%，p=0.82），但导致代码量增长12.8%（p=0.003），使得架构坏味密度下降6.7%（p=0.004）——这实际上是分母效应而非架构改进。研究警示：密度归一化指标在系统规模受处理影响时会产生误导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有因果证据仅衡量了代码层面的影响（复杂度、静态分析警告），AI编码工具是否会导致架构层面的退化尚属未知。

Method: 采用交错双重差分（staggered DiD）与Borusyak插值估计器，对151个开源Java仓库（74个检测到AI采纳+77个倾向性匹配对照）进行13个月面板分析，共采集1,811份月度Arcan快照，估算了AI采纳对架构坏味密度（ASD）的因果效应。

Result: 总体坏味数量基本不变（+1.1%，p=0.82），代码行数增加12.8%（p=0.003），导致ASD下降6.7%（p=0.004）。该下降为分母效应而非架构质量改进。多种稳健性检验（wild cluster bootstrap、Lee bounds、陈旧观测敏感性）均印证了这一模式，且前趋势平坦（Wald p=0.90）。

Conclusion: 密度归一化指标在处理影响系统规模时具有误导性；因果挖掘研究需要同时报告原始计数和显式分解。提供完整可复现的数据包。

Abstract: AI coding tools are now used by a majority of developers, and agentic use of these tools has popularized the practice colloquially called "vibe coding". Yet causal evidence on their effect on software architecture is scarce. Prior causal work has measured code-level outcomes (complexity, static analysis warnings); whether such degradation propagates to architecture-level outcomes remains unknown. We mine 151 open-source Java repositories, 74 with detectable agentic AI adoption (identified via configuration files and Co-Authored-By commit trailers) and 77 propensity-matched controls, across a 13-month per-repository window yielding 1,811 monthly Arcan snapshots. We estimate the causal effect of adoption on architectural smell density (ASD) with a staggered difference-in-differences design and the Borusyak imputation estimator, applying a causal design recently used for code-level metrics to the architecture level. Total smell counts are essentially unchanged (+1.1%, p = 0.82) while lines of code grow +12.8% (p = 0.003); the resulting 6.7% ASD decline (p = 0.004) is therefore a denominator effect rather than an architectural improvement. Per-type estimates and robustness checks (wild cluster bootstrap, Lee bounds, stale-observation sensitivity) corroborate the pattern; pre-trends are flat (Wald p = 0.90), consistent with parallel trends. Density-normalized outcomes can mislead when treatment affects system size: raw counts and explicit decomposition are required for causal mining studies of AI tool adoption. The complete replication package, including the curated 151-repository monthly panel, is publicly available.

</details>


### [215] [Toward Instructions-as-Code: Understanding the Impact of Instruction Files on Agentic Pull Requests](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13449)
*Ali Arabat,Mohammed Sayagh*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文分析了15,549个AI智能体PR（来自148个项目），发现为AI智能体创建指令文件并不总能提升PR合并率、处理复杂任务能力或降低合并工作量。约27.7%的项目合并率提升超20%，但26.35%的项目反而下降。成功提升合并率的项目通常拥有更长、结构更清晰的指令文件。研究呼吁将指令文件开发视为软件工程活动（指令即代码）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究AI智能体指令文件的创建与智能体在创建PR时的性能之间的关系，具体考察指令文件是否有助于提高PR合并率、处理更复杂任务以及降低合并所需的工作量。

Method: 基于AIDev数据集，分析来自148个项目的15,549个AI智能体PR，从合并率、代码变更量、合并工作量三个维度，比较各项目在创建指令文件前后的性能差异。

Result: 指令文件并未必然带来更好的结果：27.7%的项目合并率提升超20%，26.35%的项目下降；代码变更量和合并工作量方面也呈现类似的两极分化现象；成功提升合并率的项目拥有更长且结构更清晰的指令文件。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了指令文件对AI智能体性能影响的复杂性，并呼吁将指令文件的开发视为一项正式的软件工程活动（Instructions-as-Code），以指导实践者更好地编写指令。

Abstract: AI-agents (e.g., GitHub Copilot) collaborate as teammates in different software engineering tasks, including code generation proposed through pull requests (Agentic-PRs). For better agent efficiency, developers create instruction files that guide the AI-agents, including how to navigate the project, locate the right components, run tests, respect best practices, and more. In this paper, we investigate the relationship between the creation of these instructions and the performance of AI-agents in creating better pull requests, which have a higher chance of success (i.e., the merge rate), address more complex tasks (e.g., code churn), and require less effort to be merged (e.g., time to merge). To this end, we analyze 15,549 agentic PRs from 148 projects in the AIDev dataset. Using the three dimensions, we compare each project before and after the creation of the instruction files. We find that specifying instructions for AI-agents does not necessarily lead to better results. With the instruction files, 27.7\% of the projects increased their merge rate by at least 20\%, while 26.35\% decreased it. The same observation is seen with the amount of changes (e.g., code churn, number of modified files) and with the efforts to merge an agentic PR (e.g., merge time and number of comments). From a first exploration, we find that projects that managed to increase their merge rate have substantially longer instruction files, which are also well structured into a higher number of sections and sub-sections. Our results motivate the need for research to assist practitioners in framing the development of instruction files as a software engineering activity (aka, \textbf{Instructions-as-Code}).

</details>


### [216] [Understanding the Rejection of Fixes Generated by Agentic Pull Requests -- Insights from the AIDev Dataset](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13468)
*Mahmoud Abujadallah,Ali Arabat,Mohammed Sayagh*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过对AIDev数据集的首次探索发现，Copilot、Devin、Cursor和Claude等AI编码智能体生成的PR修复中，46.41%被拒绝。作者对306个未合并PR进行定性研究，识别出14个拒绝原因，分为四大类：实现不正确、未通过CI流水线、无法执行实现、优先级低。研究建议在方法提示、约束限制和CI验证三个层面改进AI智能体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI编码智能体生成的代码修复有近半数被拒绝，造成大量人力资源和计算资源的浪费。理解AI智能体的失败模式对于更好地将其整合为高效团队成员至关重要。

Method: 对AIDev数据集中Copilot、Devin、Cursor和Claude创建的306个未合并PR（即被拒绝的修复）进行定性研究，随后进行拒绝原因的定量分析。

Result: 识别出14个具体拒绝原因，归纳为四大类别：(1) 实现不正确（不完整、方法错误等）；(2) 未通过CI流水线和测试；(3) 无法执行实现（未生成代码、会话丢失等）；(4) 修复优先级低。

Conclusion: 需从三个层面改进AI智能体：提供修复方法的提示、明确不应采用的方法约束、指导CI验证方式。同时需要对任务进行良好的优先级排序，避免浪费人工审查和智能体资源。

Abstract: AI coding agents are increasingly used to generate pull requests (PRs) that propose code fixes in software projects. From a first exploration of the AIDev dataset, we find that 46.41\% of the fixes proposed by the agents Copilot, Devin, Cursor, and Claude are rejected. This represents a significant amount of wasted resources that require human reviews, verifications, and running tests and validations for fixes that are merely discarded. Our goal in this paper is to understand the failure modes of AI-agents, an understanding that is crucial for better integrating AI-agents as efficient teammates. In this paper, we conduct a qualitative study on a representative sample of 306 non-merged pull requests created or co-authored by the agents mentioned earlier, followed by a quantitative analysis of the reasons for rejection. Our qualitative findings identify 14 reasons divided into four high-level categories for rejecting AI-agent fixes. We observe that developers can reject fixes due to fixes whose implementation is incorrect (e.g., incomplete, wrong approach), fixes that do not pass the continuous integration (CI) pipelines and fail tests, fixes for which the agent is unable to perform the implementation (e.g., no code generated, sessions lost), and fixes whose priority is low. Our results shed light on the importance of better guiding the model at these levels: (1) proposing hints about the approach to follow for fixing an issue, (2) outlining constraints or limitations regarding the approaches that should not be taken, and (3) instructing the agent on how to validate the implementation through CI pipelines and without introducing a breaking change. Our results suggest the need for good prioritization of tasks so that generated fixes do not lead to wasted human review efforts or wasted agent resources (e.g., tokens, compute, or allowed number of requests).

</details>

### [217] [Trait, Not State: The Durability of Reading Identity in Social Highlighting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12904)
*Kazuki Nakayashiki,Keisuke Watanabe*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文通过追踪读者在社交网页高亮选择上的长期数据，探究个人选择签名是稳定特质还是可变的短期状态。研究发现，读者在长达24个月以上的时间跨度内，其选择签名保持高度稳定，细粒度层面的优势无统计显著衰退，且该信号不能被重复域名解释。个人档案在预测未来选择时表现优于所有非个性化基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究仅从横截面角度发现个体在高亮选择上的独特性，但未考察这种独特性是否随时间保持稳定。本文旨在回答一个时间性问题：读者的选择签名究竟是一种稳定的特质（trait），还是一种可变的短期状态（state）？

Method: 研究将每位读者前六个月的高亮行为冻结为个人档案，随后追踪这些档案与其后续选择（间隔从6个月到24个月以上）的自他匹配优势。负样本取自同一日历时期以避免供应漂移干扰。实验在粗粒度（全局）和细粒度（读者自身兴趣邻域内）两个层面进行，并验证了与先前横截面研究结果的一致性（+0.188 vs +0.169）。

Result: 四个主要结果：（1）细粒度层面的自他优势在任何时间间隔内均无统计显著的配对下降（6-12个月保留率R=1.00 [0.85, 1.18]）；（2）信号不能归因于重复域名（排除后仍保留约90%）；（3）个人档案内的漂移缓慢（近期半年档案比旧档案仅好+0.042）；（4）前瞻性实验中，个人档案在预测下一篇文章时的平均精度（AP）约为所有简单非个性化基线的3倍。

Conclusion: 在持续参与的条件下，读者的选择签名表现为一种稳定特质而非短期状态。但该结论限于一个平台上的长期重度读者群体，且无法区分曝光效应与主动选择。

Abstract: Prior work on a social web highlighter located individuality in selection -- which documents a person chooses to highlight -- but measured it cross-sectionally. We ask the temporal question: is a reader's selection signature a trait or a state? We freeze each reader's first six months of highlighting as a profile and track its own-vs-other advantage on their later selections at growing gaps (to 24+ months), with negatives drawn from the same calendar era -- so supply drift cannot masquerade as personal drift -- at a coarse global level and at a fine level whose negatives and controls come from the reader's own interest neighborhood; the anchor cell reproduces the prior cross-sectional level (+0.188 vs +0.169), validating the harness. Four results. Within the same users, the fine-layer advantage shows no statistically detectable paired decline at any horizon (6-12 month retention R = 1.00 [0.85, 1.18], n = 212; the farthest bin is compatible with a modest decline; the only contrast whose interval excludes zero is the coarse layer at 12-24 months, about 13%). The signal is not reducible to repeated domains (~90% survives excluding all profile sources). Within-person drift is slow (a recent-half profile beats the old half by +0.042). Prospectively, personal profiles -- even one built from a reader's earliest documents, median 20 months before evaluation -- rank their next reads at roughly 3x the AP of every simple non-personal prior tested. We use "trait" operationally (a stable signature under continued engagement); the scope is heavy, long-tenured readers of one platform, and exposure is not separable from choice.

</details>


### [218] [Charge as a Construct-Validity Factor in Chinese Legal Case Retrieval: A Cross-Benchmark Audit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12993)
*Yao Liu,Tien-Ping Tan,Zhilan Liu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 法律案例检索基准LeCaRDv2中，仅通过共有主要罪名排序（辅以BM25断链）即可恢复BM25与最佳训练模型之间99.2%的差距，揭示基准设计中的罪名构造效度问题。罪名是高水平构造效度因素，并非NDCG@10的统一解释，也不表明任何系统依赖罪名。我们发布可复用的罪名控制协议（CCE）用于筛查未来基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有法律案例检索基准中，训练模型相对于BM25的巨大提升可能主要来自基准设计本身对罪名的依赖（罪名相同的案例天然相关），而非模型真正的法律推理能力。作者希望揭示并量化这一构造效度混淆因素。

Method: 1. 在LeCaRDv2上，仅基于共有主要罪名排序（不训练任何检索模型），用BM25在同罪名组内断链；2. 在LeCaRDv1和CAIL2022上重复验证；3. 使用预测罪名级联分析跨基准迁移性；4. 提出罪名控制协议（CCE）作为可复用的构造效度筛查工具；5. 使用聚类自助法（cluster-bootstrap）进行统计推断。

Result: 1. 仅共享主要罪名排序+BM25断链关闭了BM25与最佳模型间99.2%的差距（LeCaRDv2），且与最佳模型无统计学可检测差异；2. 固定罪名后，训练重排器相对于BM25的优势仅为+0.026 NDCG@10（约四分之一）；3. 同一规则在LeCaRDv1上恢复84.3%，在CAIL2022上不符合规格；4. 罪名与相关性的macro-AUC依次为0.871/0.759/0.728，与恢复比例一致；5. 零训练罪名池通道提升LeCaRDv2的R@100 +0.025。

Conclusion: 法律案例检索基准存在严重的构造效度问题——罪名是相关性的高杠杆预测因子，导致NDCG@10分数主要反映的是罪名匹配而非法律推理能力。作者呼吁未来基准在使用NDCG@10作为法律推理能力的指标前，应先进行构造效度筛查。

Abstract: Chinese Legal Case Retrieval (LCR) benchmarks grade a reference judgment relevant when its legal characterization matches the query, and strong systems now reach NDCG@10 of 0.85-0.88. Most of the BM25-to-best-trained gap is recoverable with no retrieval model: ranking candidates only by shared primary charge, broken by BM25, closes 99.2% of it on LeCaRDv2 -- with no detectable difference from the best-trained system. This reflects benchmark design: LeCaRDv2 defines top relevance via the crime's key constitutive elements, which encode the charge, so same-charge cases are relevant by construction (relevance lift 4.49; charge-to-relevance macro-AUC 0.871). Holding charge fixed, the trained reranker's advantage over BM25 collapses to a small within-charge residual (+0.026 NDCG@10, cluster-bootstrap CI excluding zero, about a quarter), the only non-definitional positive. The effect is not uniform: the same rule recovers 84.3% on LeCaRDv1 and is out of spec on CAIL2022, with the charge-to-relevance signal weakening in step (macro-AUC 0.871/0.759/0.728); a predicted-charge cascade reproduces 76.6% on LeCaRDv2 but does not transfer. The construct is also cashable at first stage: an exploratory zero-training charge-pool channel lifts LeCaRDv2 recall (R@100 +0.025, wrong-charge controls hurt), reported as a positive control for the confound, not a retrieval method or novelty claim. Charge is thus a high-leverage construct-validity factor at the benchmark level -- not auniform explanation of NDCG@10, and not evidence that any system relies on charge. We package established construct-validity and partial-input checks as a reusable charge-controlled protocol (CCE); on all three benchmarks its triggers come back null or descriptive, behaving as designed. We release the scripts, schema, and protocol so future benchmarks can be screened before their NDCG@10 is read as legal-reasoning ability.

</details>

Conclusion: CFALR成功弥合了协同过滤与大型语言模型之间的鸿沟，为个性化服装推荐提供了一种高效且有效的解决方案，在数据稀疏场景下具有显著优势。

Abstract: Personalized outfit recommendation poses a significant challenge in e-commerce and social media platforms, requiring systems that balance user preferences with aesthetic compatibility. Meanwhile, existing template-based approaches are constrained by rigid pre-designed structures. To bridge these research gaps, we introduce CFALR (Collaborative Filtering-Augmented Large Language Model for Recommendation), a novel framework that synergizes collaborative filtering with large language models for personalized outfit recommendation. Specifically, CFALR describes user-outfit interactions in natural language and leverages LLMs to capture fashion semantics while employing CF-enhanced embeddings to bridge the semantic space and the collaborative interaction spaces. Our technical contributions include: (1) the first LLM-based architecture specifically designed for personalized outfit recommendation, (2) a CF-augmented generative mechanism that efficiently navigates the extensive combination space of outfit items, and (3) trainable projection layers that optimally integrate relational and content features. Experiments on Polyvore and IQON benchmarks demonstrate CFALR's superior performance over both traditional CF-based and LLM-based methods in personalized fill-in-the-blank and personalized outfit generation tasks.

### [220] [The Clustering Strikes Back: Building Cost-Effective and High-Performance ANNS at Scale with Helmsman](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13145)
*Yuchen Huang,Baiteng Ma,Yiping Sun,Yang Shi,Xiao Chen,Xiaocheng Zhong,Zhiyong Wang,Yao Hu,Erci Xu,Chuliang Weng*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: HELMSMAN 是一个基于全闪存服务器的高性能、低成本聚类ANNS系统，通过ANNS导向的用户态存储栈、层级学习式剪枝模块和GPU加速构建流水线，在保持高性能的同时节省超90%硬件成本，实现40台机器替代原先约35,000核和0.35 PB DRAM的生产部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小红书采用内存图式ANNS（HNSW）支撑搜索、推荐和广告服务，但用户和内容持续增长导致内存占用爆炸式增长，带来巨大的资本支出和运营成本。需要探索更经济的替代方案。

Method: 1) ANNS导向的用户态存储栈，避免内核I/O栈开销；2) 层级学习式剪枝模块，替代固定剪枝策略；3) GPU加速的构建流水线，加速索引构建与重建。

Result: 节省超90%硬件成本，支持十亿级索引在数小时内构建/重建，生产环境稳定运行数月，40台机器承载原需约35,000核和0.35 PB DRAM的ANNS工作负载。

Conclusion: 基于全闪存服务器的聚类ANNS方案可大幅降低大规模ANNS部署的硬件成本，通过精心设计的系统优化（用户态存储、学习式剪枝、GPU加速）可在保证性能的同时实现数量级的成本节约。

Abstract: RedNote (a.k.a., Xiaohongshu, a global-scale social network platform) widely adopts approximate nearest neighbor search (ANNS) to power its search, recommendation, and advertising services. Due to the demanding Service Level Agreements (SLAs), we have to rely on in-memory graph-based ANNS (i.e., HNSW) to provide high throughput and low latency.
  However, the ever-growing user base and content volume have led to an explosive increase in memory footprint and consequently huge CapEx and OpEx. After exploring various alternatives, we find that building a clustering-based ANNS on top of all-flash servers can be promising. Yet, we still experience severe overheads from the kernel I/O stack, a fixed pruning strategy, and slow index construction.
  We present HELMSMAN, a high-performance and cost-effective clustering-based ANNS system, which combines an ANNS-oriented userspace storage stack, a leveling-learned pruning module, and GPU-accelerated pipelines of construction. HELMSMAN saves over 90% of hardware costs and enables billion-scale index (re)builds within hours. In the current production deployment, operating stably for several months, 40 machines now host ANNS workloads that previously required about 35,000 cores and 0.35 PB DRAM.

### [221] [CoDeR: Local Constraint-Compatible Retrieval Beyond Semantic Similarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13204)
*Xingkun Yin,Xuebin Tang,Hongyang Du*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对约束敏感查询中语义相似度作为相关性代理的失效问题（即文档与查询主题相近但支持相反约束方向），本文提出CoDeR方法，通过分离主题相关性（标准编码器）与约束兼容性（双编码器，基于词汇极性监督训练），在不依赖外部LLM的情况下重新排序或检索兼容性候选集。在反义、否定、排除三类受控诊断集上，V@2相对降低20.59、23.53和5.77点，并提升了首个违规文档的排名位置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统信息检索系统将语义相似度作为相关性的代理，但对于约束敏感查询（如排除某属性或否定某关系），这一代理可能失效：文档与查询主题相近却支持相反的约束方向（即约束违规证据暴露）。现有方法未能明确分离主题相关性与约束兼容性，导致排名结果包含违规文档。

Method: CoDeR包含两个组件：（1）标准主题编码器用于候选覆盖；（2）约束兼容性评分器（双编码器架构），基于词汇极性监督信号在对比性满足与违规证据上训练。兼容性信号可用于重新排名主题候选集，或检索辅助的兼容性导向候选集，推理时无需外部LLM调用。

Result: 在反义、否定、排除三类受控诊断集上，CoDeR使V@2分别相对降低20.59、23.53和5.77点（优于最强非CoDeR基线），并通过将首个违规文档推至更靠后位置来提升FVR指标。

Conclusion: 分离主题相关性与约束兼容性可有效缓解约束敏感查询中的违规证据暴露问题，且无需在推理时依赖外部LLM，展示了局部约束兼容性检索的可行性与有效性。

Abstract: Information retrieval systems have long treated semantic similarity as a proxy for relevance. For constraint-sensitive queries, this proxy can fail when a document is topically close to the query but supports the opposite constraint direction, such as satisfying an attribute that should be excluded or affirming a relation that should be negated. We study this failure as constraint-violating evidence exposure and propose CoDeR, a local constraint-compatible dense retrieval method that separates topical relevance from constraint compatibility. CoDeR keeps a standard topical encoder for candidate coverage and adds a compatibility scorer, implemented as a bi-encoder, trained with lexical-polarity supervision over contrastive satisfying and violating evidences. The compatibility signal can be used to rescore topical candidates or to retrieve an auxiliary compatibility-oriented candidate set, producing a ranked document list without external Large Language Model~(LLM) calls at inference time. We evaluate CoDeR on controlled diagnostics and public negative-constraint retrieval benchmarks. Across three controlled diagnostic sets targeting antonymy, negation, and exclusion, CoDeR reduces V@2 by 20.59, 23.53, and 5.77 points relative to the strongest non-CoDeR baselines, and improves FVR by pushing the first violating document deeper in the ranking.

</details>


### [222] [CQC-RAG: Robust Retrieval-Augmented Generation via Cross-Query Consistency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13438)
*Yanjia Sun,Sifan Liu,Jie Shao*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出基于跨查询一致性假设的CQC-RAG框架，通过将原始问题改写为语义等价但句法多样的多个查询，并在共享文档池上进行重排序构建查询条件推理上下文，利用答案在不同上下文间的置信度稳定性来过滤噪声引发的幻觉，在四个开放域问答数据集上超越现有基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG方法对检索证据的可靠性敏感，多路径推理方法虽能提升鲁棒性，但存在两个局限：多样性仅通过不可控的解码随机性注入，且答案评估局限于单一查询引发的证据视图。需要一种能主动注入多样性并在跨查询间进行一致性评估的方法。

Method: 提出跨查询一致性假设（正确答案在不同句法形式但语义等价的查询下保持高置信度，幻觉答案则不稳定）；构建CQC-RAG框架，包含：1）查询改写生成多样性查询；2）共享文档池重排序构建查询条件推理上下文；3）基于证据的答案-证据对提取协议；4）跨上下文置信度稳定性评估选择答案。

Result: 在四个开放域问答基准上，CQC-RAG超越最强多查询基线：TriviaQA上+4.76 pp EM，MuSiQue上+9.12 pp EM，验证了跨查询一致性对过滤噪声引发幻觉的有效性。

Conclusion: 跨查询一致性是一种有效的无需外部监督的自评估机制，能显著提升RAG系统的事实性；该方法不依赖扩展检索覆盖范围，而是通过查询级多样性注入与跨查询一致性评估的协同设计实现噪声过滤。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has become a common approach for improving the factuality of Large Language Models (LLMs), yet its reliability remains highly sensitive to how external evidence is retrieved and used. Semantically equivalent queries with different syntactic forms may lead to different retrieval results, while irrelevant or misleading documents can further induce hallucinated answers. Existing multi-path reasoning methods improve robustness by sampling multiple candidate answers and applying voting- or confidence-based selection, but they still face two limitations: diversity is often injected through uncontrollable decoding randomness, and answer evaluation is usually confined to a single query-induced evidence view. To address these limitations, we propose a Cross-Query Consistency Hypothesis: correct answers tend to maintain high confidence across semantically equivalent but syntactically diverse queries, whereas noise-induced hallucinations exhibit unstable confidence under such query variations. Based on this hypothesis, we introduce CQC-RAG, a framework that co-designs query-level diversity injection with cross-query consistency evaluation. CQC-RAG rewrites the original question into diverse but meaning-preserving queries, reranks a shared document pool to construct query-conditioned reasoning contexts, applies an evidence-grounded protocol to extract answer-evidence pairs and selects answers according to their confidence stability across these contexts. This design enables self-evaluation without external supervision and does not rely on expanded retrieval coverage. Experiments on four open-domain question answering benchmarks show that CQC-RAG outperforms the strongest previous multi-query baseline by +4.76 pp EM on TriviaQA and +9.12 pp EM on MuSiQue, validating the effectiveness of cross-query consistency for filtering noise-induced hallucinations.

</details>


### [223] [OneRetrieval: Unifying Multi-Branch E-commerce Retrieval with an Editable Generative Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13533)
*Xuxin Zhang,Ben Chen,Yue Lv,Siyuan Wang,Yupeng Li,Yufei Ma,Zihan Liang,Tong Zhao,Ying Yang,Huangyu Dai,Lingtao Mao,Zhipeng Qian,Xinyu Sun,Chenyi Lei,Wenwu Ou,Kun Gai*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出OneRetrieval，一种支持实时编辑的生成式检索框架，通过关键词对齐编码（KAE）将每个标识符位置与可解释属性词绑定，在保持竞争性召回质量的同时实现倒排索引级别的可编辑性，已在快手部署并显著提升业务指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业电商搜索的多分支检索阶段依赖手工调参融合，缺乏联合优化。生成式检索（GR）有望将多分支合并为单一模型，但现有GR方法缺乏实时可编辑性——倒排索引分支虽召回率低于平台平均水平，却是唯一能通过运营操作在数小时内注入新词而无需模型更新的分支。需要一个既能保持良好召回质量又能保留实时编辑能力的统一模型。

Method: OneRetrieval框架包含：（1）关键词对齐编码（KAE），将每个标识符位置绑定到可解释属性词；（2）信息论合并策略，将18个属性类别组织为6个非均匀容量的码本组；（3）每个码本中预留槽位，可在部署后绑定新词而无需重新训练；（4）四阶段微调流水线，联合保障质量和可编辑性。

Result: 在五百万真实流量请求上，OneRetrieval的深度召回达到最强生成式基线水平，干预命中率比闭码本编码高一个数量级以上。线上替换倒排索引分支显著提升订单量；扩展到几乎整个检索阶段可保持转化率同时提升点击率。

Conclusion: OneRetrieval是首个支持实时编辑的生成式检索方法，成功在单一模型中统一了多分支检索，既保持了竞争性的召回质量，又保留了倒排索引的实时可编辑性。系统已在快手部署，服务每日数亿PV。

Abstract: Industrial e-commerce search serves hundreds of millions of items through a multi-branch retrieval stage fused by hand-tuned merging without joint optimization. Generative retrieval (GR) raises the prospect of collapsing this stage into a single model, yet unification is gated by more than retrieval quality: the inverted-index branch converts below the platform average yet persists because it is almost the only branch where operations can inject a new term within hours without any model update; a one-model substitute must preserve this real-time editability. Existing GR methods structurally lack it: closed-codebook methods fix each slot to a quantized embedding at training, while open-vocabulary methods leave new-term routing to model generalization. We present OneRetrieval, a one-model GR framework built on Keyword-Aligned Encoding (KAE), which ties each identifier position to an interpretable attribute word, pairing competitive recall quality with the editability of the inverted index -- to our knowledge the first editable generative retrieval method. An information-theoretic merging organizes 18 attribute categories into six codebook groups with non-uniform capacity; reserved slots in each codebook can be bound to new words after deployment without retraining; and a four-stage fine-tuning pipeline secures quality and editability jointly. On five million real-traffic requests, OneRetrieval matches the deep recall of the strongest generative baseline, with an intervention hit rate over an order of magnitude above closed-codebook encodings. Online, replacing the inverted-index branch significantly lifts order volume; extending to nearly the entire stage holds conversion while improving CTR. The system is deployed at Kuaishou, serving hundreds of millions of PVs daily.

</details>
